# Utility Class Reference

This document classifies the utility classes by CSS property groups.
It focuses on naming patterns (not an exhaustive list of every class).
For deeper, section-by-section detail, see:
- projects/kyrolus-sous-materials/CHEATSHEET.md
- projects/kyrolus-sous-materials/DOCUMENTATION.md

## Scales and Naming

### Spacing scale keys
0, px, 0.5, 1, 1.5, 2, 2.5, 3, 3.5, 4, 5, 6, 7, 8, 9, 10, 11, 12,
14, 16, 20, 24, 28, 32, 36, 40, 44, 48, 52, 56, 60, 64, 72, 80, 96

### Breakpoint prefixes
xs, sm, md, lg, xl, 2xl, 3xl
Usage example: `md:w-1/2`, `lg:px-8`

### Container query prefixes
@xs, @sm, @md, @lg, @xl, @2xl, @3xl, @4xl, @5xl
Usage example: `@sm:grid-cols-2`

### Color palettes (shades 50..950)
slate, gray, zinc, neutral, stone, red, orange, amber, yellow, lime, green,
emerald, teal, cyan, sky, blue, indigo, violet, purple, fuchsia, pink, rose

## Spacing

### Padding
`p-*`, `px-*`, `py-*`, `pt-*`, `pr-*`, `pb-*`, `pl-*`,
`ps-*`, `pe-*`, `pi-*`, `pbs-*`, `pbe-*`, `pb-logical-*`

### Margin
`m-*`, `mx-*`, `my-*`, `mt-*`, `mr-*`, `mb-*`, `ml-*`,
`ms-*`, `me-*`, `mi-*`, `mbs-*`, `mbe-*`, `mb-logical-*`

### Negative margin
`-m-*`, `-mt-*`, `-mr-*`, `-mb-*`, `-ml-*`, `-mx-*`, `-my-*`

### Auto margin
`m-auto`, `mx-auto`, `my-auto`, `mt-auto`, `mr-auto`, `mb-auto`, `ml-auto`,
`ms-auto`, `me-auto`

### Gap and space-between
`gap-*`, `gap-x-*`, `gap-y-*`, `space-x-*`, `space-y-*`,
`space-x-reverse`, `space-y-reverse`

## Sizing

### Width
`w-*`, `w-1/2`, `w-1/3`, `w-2/3`, `w-1/4`, `w-3/4`, `w-full`,
`w-auto`, `w-screen`, `w-dvw`, `w-svw`, `w-lvw`, `w-min`, `w-max`, `w-fit`

### Height
`h-*`, `h-1/2`, `h-1/3`, `h-2/3`, `h-1/4`, `h-3/4`, `h-full`,
`h-auto`, `h-screen`, `h-dvh`, `h-svh`, `h-lvh`, `h-min`, `h-max`, `h-fit`

### Min/Max
`min-w-*`, `max-w-*`, `min-h-*`, `max-h-*`

### Size (width + height)
`size-*`, `size-auto`, `size-full`, `size-min`, `size-max`, `size-fit`

## Layout and Display

### Display
`hidden`, `block`, `inline`, `inline-block`, `flex`, `inline-flex`,
`grid`, `inline-grid`, `table`, `inline-table`, `table-row`, `table-cell`,
`flow-root`, `contents`, `list-item`

### Flexbox
`flex-row`, `flex-col`, `flex-row-reverse`, `flex-col-reverse`
`flex-wrap`, `flex-nowrap`, `flex-wrap-reverse`
`flex-1`, `flex-auto`, `flex-initial`, `flex-none`
`grow`, `grow-0`, `shrink`, `shrink-0`
`basis-*`
`items-*`, `justify-*`, `content-*`, `self-*`, `place-items-*`,
`place-content-*`, `place-self-*`
`order-first`, `order-last`, `order-none`, `order-1..12`

### Grid
`grid-cols-1..12`, `grid-rows-1..6`, `grid-cols-none`, `grid-rows-none`,
`grid-cols-subgrid`, `grid-rows-subgrid`
`col-span-*`, `row-span-*`, `col-start-*`, `col-end-*`, `row-start-*`, `row-end-*`
`col-auto`, `row-auto`

## Positioning

### Position
`static`, `relative`, `absolute`, `fixed`, `sticky`

### Inset and offsets
`inset-*`, `inset-x-*`, `inset-y-*`, `top-*`, `right-*`, `bottom-*`, `left-*`
`start-*`, `end-*`
Negative: `-inset-*`, `-top-*`, `-right-*`, `-bottom-*`, `-left-*`

### Z-index
`z-auto`, `z-0`, `z-10`, `z-20`, `z-30`, `z-40`, `z-50`,
`z-dropdown`, `z-sticky`, `z-fixed`, `z-backdrop`, `z-modal`, `z-popover`,
`z-tooltip`, `z-toast`, `z-max`

## Overflow and Scroll

`overflow-auto`, `overflow-hidden`, `overflow-visible`, `overflow-scroll`, `overflow-clip`
`overflow-x-*`, `overflow-y-*`
`overflow-inline-*`, `overflow-block-*`

## Typography

### Font size
`text-{xs,sm,base,lg,xl,2xl..9xl}`
`text-fluid-{xs..9xl,display,display-sm,display-lg,display-xl,display-2xl}`

### Font family
`font-sans`, `font-serif`, `font-mono`

### Font weight
`font-thin` .. `font-black`

### Line height and tracking
`leading-*`, `tracking-*`

### Alignment and transform
`text-left`, `text-center`, `text-right`, `text-justify`, `text-start`, `text-end`
`uppercase`, `lowercase`, `capitalize`

### Decoration and truncation
`underline`, `line-through`, `no-underline`, `underline-offset-*`
`text-ellipsis`, `text-clip`, `text-wrap`, `text-nowrap`, `text-balance`, `text-pretty`
`line-clamp-*`, `line-clamp-none`
`italic`, `not-italic`

## Colors

### Palette colors
`bg-{palette}-{shade}`, `text-{palette}-{shade}`, `border-{palette}-{shade}`
`ring-{palette}-{shade}`, `accent-{palette}-{shade}`, `caret-{palette}-{shade}`
`fill-{palette}-{shade}`, `stroke-{palette}-{shade}`, `decoration-{palette}-{shade}`
`placeholder-{palette}-{shade}`, `divide-{palette}-{shade}`, `outline-{palette}-{shade}`

### Semantic colors
`bg-primary`, `text-primary`, `border-primary`, `ring-primary`, etc.
`bg-secondary`, `bg-accent`, `bg-success`, `bg-warning`, `bg-danger`, `bg-info`
`text-on-primary`, `text-on-secondary`, `text-on-danger`, ...

## Borders and Radius

### Border widths
`border`, `border-0`, `border-2`, `border-4`, `border-8`
Directional: `border-t`, `border-r`, `border-b`, `border-l`, `border-x`, `border-y`,
`border-s`, `border-e`

### Border styles
`border-solid`, `border-dashed`, `border-dotted`, `border-double`, `border-none`

### Radius
`rounded-*`, `rounded-t-*`, `rounded-r-*`, `rounded-b-*`, `rounded-l-*`,
`rounded-tl-*`, `rounded-tr-*`, `rounded-bl-*`, `rounded-br-*`,
`rounded-ss-*`, `rounded-se-*`, `rounded-es-*`, `rounded-ee-*`

## Effects and Filters

### Shadows
`shadow-xs`, `shadow-sm`, `shadow`, `shadow-md`, `shadow-lg`, `shadow-xl`,
`shadow-2xl`, `shadow-inner`, `shadow-none`

### Opacity
`opacity-*`

### Blur and filters
`blur-*`, `backdrop-blur-*`, `brightness-*`, `contrast-*`, `grayscale-*`,
`hue-rotate-*`, `invert-*`, `saturate-*`, `sepia-*`

### Gradients
`bg-gradient-to-*`, `bg-gradient-radial*`, `bg-gradient-conic*`
`from-*`, `via-*`, `to-*`

## Animation and Transition

### Animation
`animate-*` (spin, pulse, bounce, fade, slide, zoom, flip, etc.)
`duration-*`, `delay-*`, `ease-*`, `animate-once`, `animate-infinite`,
`animate-reverse`, `animate-alternate`, `animate-fill-*`, `animate-paused`

### Transition
`transition-none`, `transition-all`, `transition-colors`, `transition-opacity`,
`transition-shadow`, `transition-transform`
`transition-duration-*`, `transition-delay-*`, `transition-*`

## State Variants

`hover:*`, `focus:*`, `active:*`, `disabled:*`, `dark:*`
Group and peer variants:
`group-hover:*`, `group-focus:*`, `group-focus-within:*`, `group-active:*`
`peer-checked:*`, `peer-focus:*`, `peer-hover:*`, `peer-disabled:*`,
`peer-invalid:*`, `peer-valid:*`, `peer-placeholder-shown:*`,
`peer-not-placeholder-shown:*`

## Component Theme Modifiers

These are scoped modifiers used by components (not global utilities):

- Table: `.advanced-table.light`, `.advanced-table.dark`
- Table layout: `.advanced-table.compact`, `.advanced-table.comfortable`, `.advanced-table.full-width`
- Paginator: `.paginator.light`, `.paginator.dark`

## Theming Summary (Quick)

Compile-time:
Use `@use ".../styles" with ($ks-*)` to set core tokens.

Runtime:
Override CSS variables under `[data-theme="custom"]` or any container.

## Where to Learn More

- docs/FRAMEWORK.md (architecture and theming)
- projects/kyrolus-sous-materials/CHEATSHEET.md (compact class summary)
- projects/kyrolus-sous-materials/DOCUMENTATION.md (full reference)
